ValueSet:       GeneticTestMethodVS
Description:    "The method used to perform a genetic test, drawn from NCI Thesaurus. Examples include Fluorescent in situ hybridization (FISH), polymerase chain reaction-based assays (PCR), and next-generation sequencing (NGS).

FHIR is currently unable to handle values from NCI Thesaurus, so no values are listed in the Expansion, below. The values ARE in the downloads. For convenience, here is a listing of values in this value set:
